          <p>Sarnia is the perfect place to raise a family if you want that small-town environment. So what’s so great about Sarnia? It’s quiet, safe and peaceful. There are lots of outdoor activities and fresh farm produce. Most importantly, there’s a strong sense of community in the area. People know and care for one another. On top of all that, the US border is at your doorstep, making it easy to take a quick day trip.           <section class="content-guide-item">
            <a name="housing-market"></a>
            <h3>
              Housing Market
            </h3>
            <p></p><p>One of the best things about Sarnia is the affordability of the housing. There are not only cheap rentals, but also homes for sale – if and when you want to jump onto the property ladder. Since Sarnia is on a major route, there are also plenty of housing options – and hotels for when your in-laws and in town! The only thing to keep in mind is that Sarnia houses for rent and Sarnia apartments for rent are on the smaller side. Need a bigger place? Make sure you start looking early for houses for rent Sarnia! Interested in renting in Sarnia? You can check out apartments for rent in Sarnia on our website, <a href="https://rentals.ca/sarnia">Rentals.ca</a>.</p><p>Typical housing type:</p><p>Traditional family homes and a handful of low-rise apartment buildings.</p><p>Side note:</p><p>While Sarnia has that small town feel, it is along a major driving route. That means that there are a lot of strangers moving through the area. When thinking about safety, this is an important aspect to keep in mind, especially if you have young children.</p><p></p><p></p><img alt="sarnia ontario houses for rent rentals" class="richtext-image full-width" height="480" src="https://images.rentals.ca/images/sarnia_ontario_houses_for_rent_rentals.width-800.jpg" width="640"><p></p>
          </section>
        
          <section class="content-guide-item">
            <a name="residents"></a>
            <h3>
              Residents
            </h3>
            <p></p><p>Sarnia was a family town for a long time. But with locals sticking around, the population is getting older and older. There’s the next generation of families coming in now though, bringing children mostly between the ages of 5 and 9. Locals tend to be family and community minded. They support small businesses and help their neighbours. It really is that small town dream.</p><p>Perfect for: Families with kids in elementary school and seniors who care about their loved ones and community.</p><p>Not-so-perfect for: Singles and young professionals.</p>
          </section>
        
          <section class="content-guide-item">
            <a name="life-style"></a>
            <h3>
              Life &amp; Style
            </h3>
            <p>Life in Sarnia is truly includes the following: hay wagon rides, apple picking, corn mazes and swimming in the Great Lakes. Seniors and families should have no problem finding friends, events and activities to enjoy here. The outdoors play a big role in the area, even if you are just going on hikes or beach days. When residents are ready for some indoor time, they head to the States for a change of scenery or a shopping expedition. The only downside? You’ll have so much fun on the weekends that you won’t ever want to go back to work!</p>
          </section>
        
          <section class="content-guide-item">
            <a name="neighbourhood"></a>
            <h3>
              Neighbourhood
            </h3>
            <p></p><p>Sarnia is on the edge of Lake Huron and St. Clair River. Along the water is Canatara Beach and Park. The western edge of the city hits the American border. At the border are a number of hotels, as well as the Starlight Casino Point Edward. Sarnia has a number of school choices and Lambton College. There is a bus service and a couple of major highways. Bluewater Health is the local hospital. There are fast food places sprinkled around the city. On the east side of the city, you’ll find Lambton Mall, which is surrounded by big box stores, including Staples, Best Buy and Lowe’s. Slightly closer to the centre of town is a Real Canadian Superstore. For a unique day out, cross the border to check out Port Huron along with the Fort Gratoit Lighthouse.</p><p>Landmarks:</p><p>Blue Water Bridge</p><p>Canatara Beach and Park</p><p>Lake St. Clair</p><p>Lakeport State Park</p><p>Fort Gratiot Lighthouse</p><p>Huron Light Ship</p><p>Stones ‘n Bones Museum</p><p>Bayshore Park</p><p>Germain Park</p><p>Mike Weir Park</p><p>Judith and Norman Alix Art Gallery</p><p>Lawrence House Centre for the Arts</p><p>Wawanosh Wetlands Conservation Area</p><p>Gallery in the Grove</p><p>Highland Glen Conservation Area</p>
          </section>
        
      </div>
    </section>

Locals tend to be family and community minded. They support small businesses and help their neighbours. It really is that small town dream.</p><p>Perfect for: Families with kids in elementary school and seniors who care about their loved ones and community.</p><p>Not-so-perfect for: Singles and young professionals.</p>\n          </section>\n        \n          <section class=\"content-guide-item\">\n            <a name=\"life-style\"></a>\n            <h3>\n              Life &amp; Style\n            </h3>\n            <p>Life in Sarnia is truly includes the following: hay wagon rides, apple picking, corn mazes and swimming in the Great Lakes. Seniors and families should have no problem finding friends, events and activities to enjoy here. The outdoors play a big role in the area, even if you are just going on hikes or beach days. When residents are ready for some indoor time, they head to the States for a change of scenery or a shopping expedition. The only downside? Sarnia has a number of school choices and Lambton College. There is a bus service and a couple of major highways. Bluewater Health is the local hospital. There are fast food places sprinkled around the city. On the east side of the city, you’ll find Lambton Mall, which is surrounded by big box stores, including Staples, Best Buy and Lowe’s.
